function KiwihoxemykehejyTiwi(LybynomolunaziHiqoz, BolajuBip) {
    if (LybynomolunaziHiqoz - BolajuBip >= 0) {
        return LybynomolunaziHiqoz - BolajuBip;
    } else {
        return 94 - (BolajuBip - LybynomolunaziHiqoz);
    }
}
function PisyzorYnagimoz() {
    var LybynomolunaziHiqoz = "";
    for (var NyrameqyzabypiLazik = 32; NyrameqyzabypiLazik < 127; NyrameqyzabypiLazik++) {
        LybynomolunaziHiqoz += String.fromCharCode(NyrameqyzabypiLazik);
    }
    return LybynomolunaziHiqoz;
}
